if you believe the content of this training will be traumatizing, please contact the office of equity & compliance at oectraining@csulb.edu <mailto:oectraining@csulb.edu> to discuss an alternative arrangement to satisfy the requirement.

although survivor stories are included, there are no graphic representations; survivor testimony is included to empower students to seek support and resources.

access and instructions

please follow the steps below to access the training:

1.	access the csulb single sign-on with your campus id number and password 
2.	select the "title ix training" yellow chiclet tile from the home menu 
3.	log into the training site using your beach id and password 
4.	you may complete the training in one session, approximately 45-60 minutes. if you choose to complete the training in multiple sessions, you may stop and save your training at any time. you will need to log back in with your beach id and password to resume the training.
5.	when you are finished, the site provides a certificate of completion. please print or save and retain a copy for your records. if you have a registration hold because of this training requirement, the hold will be removed after one full business day. please be sure to factor the 1 business day to process training completions into your registration appointment dates.

the training program is compatible with most desktop computers, laptops, tablets, and cellular devices and requires a stable internet connection. for technical service and assistance regarding training access, please contact support@getinclusive.com <mailto:%20support@getinclusive.com> 

<mailto:%20support@getinclusive.com> for university questions regarding registration holds, campus and community resources, and the title ix reporting process please contact equity & compliance at oectraining@csulb.edu <mailto:oectraining@csulb.edu>  or 562.985.8256. when contacting equity & compliance, please have the following information available:

1.	full legal name 
2.	your student identification number 
3.	next term you are expected to start classes (as some students are contacting us regarding future enrollment dates) 
4.	your contact information (phone & email) 
5.	if requesting a hold release, you must provide a copy of your completion certificate to oec via email (oectraining@csulb.edu <mailto:oectraining@csulb.edu> ) or hardcopy (foundation building, suite 160)

go beach, 

equity & compliance

oec@csulb.edu <mailto:oec@csulb.edu>

if you believe the content of this training will be traumatizing, please contact the office of equity & compliance at oectraining@csulb.edu <mailto:oectraining@csulb.edu> to discuss an alternative arrangement to satisfy the requirement.

although survivor stories are included, there are no graphic representations; survivor testimony is included to empower students to seek support and resources.

access and instructions

please follow the steps below to access the training:

1.	access the csulb single sign-on with your campus id number and password 
2.	select the "title ix training" yellow chiclet tile from the home menu 
3.	log into the training site using your beach id and password 
4.	you may complete the training in one session, approximately 45-60 minutes. if you choose to complete the training in multiple sessions, you may stop and save your training at any time. you will need to log back in with your beach id and password to resume the training.
5.	when you are finished, the site provides a certificate of completion. please print or save and retain a copy for your records. if you have a registration hold because of this training requirement, the hold will be removed after one full business day. please be sure to factor the 1 business day to process training completions into your registration appointment dates.

the training program is compatible with most desktop computers, laptops, tablets, and cellular devices and requires a stable internet connection. for technical service and assistance regarding training access, please contact support@getinclusive.com <mailto:%20support@getinclusive.com> 

<mailto:%20support@getinclusive.com> for university questions regarding registration holds, campus and community resources, and the title ix reporting process please contact equity & compliance at oectraining@csulb.edu <mailto:oectraining@csulb.edu>  or 562.985.8256. when contacting equity & compliance, please have the following information available:

1.	full legal name 
2.	your student identification number 
3.	next term you are expected to start classes (as some students are contacting us regarding future enrollment dates) 
4.	your contact information (phone & email) 
5.	if requesting a hold release, you must provide a copy of your completion certificate to oec via email (oectraining@csulb.edu <mailto:oectraining@csulb.edu> ) or hardcopy (foundation building, suite 160)

go beach, 

equity & compliance

oec@csulb.edu <mailto:oec@csulb.edu> 


 
assigned module(s):


*	title ix student training - refresher

if you believe the content of this training will be traumatizing, please contact the office of equity & compliance at oectraining@csulb.edu <mailto:oectraining@csulb.edu> to discuss an alternative arrangement to satisfy the requirement.

although survivor stories are included, there are no graphic representations; survivor testimony is included to empower students to seek support and resources.

access and instructions

please follow the steps below to access the training:

1.	access the csulb single sign-on with your campus id number and password 
2.	select the "title ix training" yellow chiclet tile from the home menu 
3.	log into the training site using your beach id and password 
4.	you may complete the training in one session, approximately 45-60 minutes. if you choose to complete the training in multiple sessions, you may stop and save your training at any time. you will need to log back in with your beach id and password to resume the training.
5.	when you are finished, the site provides a certificate of completion. please print or save and retain a copy for your records. if you have a registration hold because of this training requirement, the hold will be removed after one full business day. please be sure to factor the 1 business day to process training completions into your registration appointment dates.

the training program is compatible with most desktop computers, laptops, tablets, and cellular devices and requires a stable internet connection. for technical service and assistance regarding training access, please contact support@getinclusive.com <mailto:%20support@getinclusive.com> 

<mailto:%20support@getinclusive.com> for university questions regarding registration holds, campus and community resources, and the title ix reporting process please contact equity & compliance at oectraining@csulb.edu <mailto:oectraining@csulb.edu>  or 562.985.8256. when contacting equity & compliance, please have the following information available:

1.	full legal name 
2.	your student identification number 
3.	next term you are expected to start classes (as some students are contacting us regarding future enrollment dates) 
4.	your contact information (phone & email) 
5.	if requesting a hold release, you must provide a copy of your completion certificate to oec via email (oectraining@csulb.edu <mailto:oectraining@csulb.edu> ) or hardcopy (foundation building, suite 160)

go beach, 

equity & compliance

oec@csulb.edu <mailto:oec@csulb.edu>
